width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color: #B0E0E6; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Seventh-day_Adventist" class="mw-redirect" title="Seventh-day Adventist">Seventh-day Adventist</a> (5%)</div><div class="legend" style="-webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;page-break-inside: avoid;break-inside: avoid-column"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color: #15F4EE; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Methodist" class="mw-redirect" title="Methodist">Methodist</a> (1%)</div><div class="legend" style="-webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;page-break-inside: avoid;break-inside: avoid-column"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color: #1F75FE; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;Other <a href="/wiki/Christians" class="mw-redirect" title="Christians">Christians</a><sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;a&#93;</a></sup> (21%)</div><div class="legend" style="-webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;page-break-inside: avoid;break-inside: avoid-column"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color:Violet; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic" class="mw-redirect" title="Roman Catholic">Roman Catholic</a> (7%)</div><div class="legend" style="-webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;page-break-inside: avoid;break-inside: avoid-column"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color:Orange; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Hindu" title="Hindu">Hindu</a> (25%)</div><div class="legend" style="-webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;page-break-inside: avoid;break-inside: avoid-column"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color:Green; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Muslim" title="Muslim">Muslim</a> (7%)</div><div class="legend" style="-webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;page-break-inside: avoid;break-inside: avoid-column"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color:Red; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;Other (3%)</div><div class="legend" style="-webkit-column-break-inside: avoid;page-break-inside: avoid;break-inside: avoid-column"><span class="legend-color" style="display:inline-block; width:1.5em; height:1.5em; margin:1px 0; border:1px solid black; background-color:Black; color:black; font-size:100%; text-align:center;">&#160;</span>&#160;<a href="/wiki/Irreligious" class="mw-redirect" title="Irreligious">Irreligious</a> (3%)</div>\n</div>\n</div></div>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Religion_in_Guyana" title="Religion in Guyana">Religion in Guyana</a></div>\n<p>According to a 2002 nationwide census on religious affiliation, 57.4% of the population was <a href="/wiki/Christianity_in_Guyana#Christianity" class="mw-redirect" title="Christianity in Guyana">Christian</a>, 28.4% was <a href="/wiki/Hinduism_in_Guyana" title="Hinduism in Guyana">Hindu</a>, 7.2% was <a href="/wiki/Islam_in_Guyana" title="Islam in Guyana">Muslim</a>, 1.9% adhered to other religions, while 2.3% of the population did not profess any.<sup id="cite_ref-CENSUS2002_52-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-CENSUS2002-52">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Among Christians, most are Protestants (34.8%) or other Christian (20.8%), but there is also a minority of Roman Catholics (7.1%). Among Hindu, Vaishnavism is the major tradition. Among Muslims, Sunni are in the majority, while there are also Shia and Ahmadiyya minorities. Among other religions, the Rastafari movement, Buddhism, and the Baha\'i Faith are the most popular.\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Government_and_politics">Government and politics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Guyana&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Government and politics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Politics_of_Guyana" title="Politics of Guyana">Politics of Guyana</a></div>\n<table class="plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Refimprove" role="presentation"><tbody><tr><td class="mbox-image"><div style="width:52px"><a href="/wiki/File:Question_book-new.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/50px-Question_book-new.svg.png" width="50" height="39" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/75px-Question_book-new.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/100px-Question_book-new.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="512" data-file-height="399" /></a></div></td><td class="mbox-text"><div class="mbox-text-span">This section <b>needs additional citations for <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">verification</a></b>.<span class="hide-when-compact"> Please help <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Guyana&amp;action=edit">improve this article</a> by <a href="/wiki/Help:Introduction_to_referencing_with_Wiki_Markup/1" title="Help:Introduction to referencing with Wiki Markup/1">adding citations to reliable sources</a>. Unsourced material may be challenged and removed.</span>  <small><i>(December 2008)</i></small><small class="hide-when-compact"><i> (<a href="/wiki/Help:Maintenance_template_removal" title="Help:Maintenance template removal">Learn how and when to remove this template message</a>)</i></small></div></td></tr></tbody></table>\n<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Old_residence.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/f/f2/Old_residence.jpg/220px-Old_residence.jpg" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/f/f2/Old_residence.jpg 1.5x" data-file-width="320" data-file-height="240" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Old_residence.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The State House, Guyana\'s presidential residence</div></div></div>\n<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Cottage_of_city_Georgetown.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/44/Cottage_of_city_Georgetown.jpg/220px-Cottage_of_city_Georgetown.jpg" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/44/Cottage_of_city_Georgetown.jpg/330px-Cottage_of_city_Georgetown.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/44/Cottage_of_city_Georgetown.jpg/440px-Cottage_of_city_Georgetown.jpg 2x" data-file-width="600" data-file-height="400" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Cottage_of_city_Georgetown.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The Supreme Court of Guyana</div></div></div>\n<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Parliament_building,_Guyana.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7f/Parliament_building%2C_Guyana.jpg/220px-Parliament_building%2C_Guyana.jpg" width="220" height="128" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7f/Parliament_building%2C_Guyana.jpg/330px-Parliament_building%2C_Guyana.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7f/Parliament_building%2C_Guyana.jpg/440px-Parliament_building%2C_Guyana.jpg 2x" data-file-width="701" data-file-height="409" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Parliament_building,_Guyana.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Guyana\'s parliament building since 1834</div></div></div>\n<p>The <a href="/wiki/Politics_of_Guyana" title="Politics of Guyana">politics of Guyana</a> takes place in a framework of a <a href="/wiki/Presidential_system" title="Presidential system">presidential</a> <a href="/wiki/Representative_democracy" title="Representative democracy">representative democratic</a> <a href="/wiki/Republic" title="Republic">republic</a>, in which the <a href="/wiki/President_of_Guyana" title="President of Guyana">President of Guyana</a> is both <a href="/wiki/Head_of_state" title="Head of state">head of state</a> and <a href="/wiki/Head_of_government" title="Head of government">head of government</a>, and of a <a href="/wiki/Multi-party_system" title="Multi-party system">multi-party system</a>. <a href="/wiki/Executive_power" class="mw-redirect" title="Executive power">Executive power</a> is exercised by the President and the Government. <a href="/wiki/Legislative_power" class="mw-redirect" title="Legislative power">Legislative power</a> is vested in both the President and the <a href="/wiki/National_Assembly_of_Guyana" class="mw-redirect" title="National Assembly of Guyana">National Assembly of Guyana</a>. Historically, politics are a source of tension in the country, and violent riots have often broken out during elections. During the 1970s and 1980s, the political landscape was dominated by the People\'s National Congress.\n</p><p>In 1992, the first "free and fair" elections were overseen by former United States President <a href="/wiki/Jimmy_Carter" title="Jimmy Carter">Jimmy Carter</a>, and the People\'s Progressive Party led the country until 2015. The two parties are principally organised along ethnic lines and as a result often clash on issues related to the allocation of resources. In the General Elections held on 28 November 2011, the People\'s Progressive Party (PPP) retained a majority, and their presidential candidate <a href="/wiki/Donald_Ramotar" title="Donald Ramotar">Donald Ramotar</a> was elected as President. On 11 May 2015, early general elections were held, resulting in a victory for A Partnership for National Unity-Alliance for Change (APNU-AFC) Coalition party. APNU-AFC, a multi-ethnic, multi-party coalition, won a majority, 33 of 65 seats in the National Assembly. On 16 May 2015, retired army general <a href="/wiki/David_A._Granger" title="David A. Granger">David A. Granger</a> became the eighth President of Guyana.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Public_procurement">Public procurement</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Guyana&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Public procurement">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<p><a href="/wiki/Government_procurement" title="Government procurement">Public procurement</a> in Guyana is overseen by the Public Procurement Commission, appointed under the Public Procurement Commission Act 2003. Due to lengthy delay in identifying and agreeing commission members, the commission was not appointed until 2016.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Military">Military</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Guyana&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Military">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Guyana_Defence_Force" title="Guyana Defence Force">Guyana Defence Force</a></div>\n<p>The Guyana Defence Force (GDF) is the military service of Guyana.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Human_rights">Human rights</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Guyana&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Human rights">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/LGBT_rights_in_Guyana" title="LGBT rights in Guyana">LGBT rights in Guyana</a></div>\n<p><a href="/wiki/Homosexuality" title="Homosexuality">Homosexual</a> acts are illegal in Guyana.<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Infrastructure_and_telecommunications">Infrastructure and telecommunications</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Guyana&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Infrastructure and telecommunications">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Transport">Transport</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Guyana&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Transport">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Transport_in_Guyana" title="Transport in Guyana">Transport in Guyana</a></div>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:LethemBridge.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/73/LethemBridge.jpg/220px-LethemBridge.jpg" width="220" height="149" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/73/LethemBridge.jpg/330px-LethemBridge.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/73/LethemBridge.jpg/440px-LethemBridge.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1050" data-file-height="713" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:LethemBridge.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Cross-border bridge from Guyana to Brazil near <a href="/wiki/Lethem,_Guyana" title="Lethem, Guyana">Lethem</a></div></div></div>\n<p>There are a total of 187 kilometres (116&#160;mi) of railway, all dedicated to ore transport. There are 7,969 kilometres (4,952&#160;mi) of highway, of which 591 kilometres (367&#160;mi) are paved. Navigable waterways extend 1,077 kilometres (669&#160;mi), including the Berbice, Demerara, and Essequibo rivers.\nThere are ports at Georgetown, Port Kaituma, and <a href="/wiki/New_Amsterdam,_Guyana" title="New Amsterdam, Guyana">New Amsterdam</a>. There are two international airports (<a href="/wiki/Cheddi_Jagan_International_Airport" title="Cheddi Jagan International Airport">Cheddi Jagan International Airport</a>, Timehri and Eugene F. Correira International Airport (formerly <a href="/wiki/Ogle_Airport" class="mw-redirect" title="Ogle Airport">Ogle Airport</a>); along with about 90 airstrips, nine of which have paved runways. Guyana, Suriname and the <a href="/wiki/Falkland_Islands" title="Falkland Islands">Falkland Islands</a> are the only three regions in South America which <a href="/wiki/Drive_on_the_left" class="mw-redirect" title="Drive on the left">drive on the left</a>.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Electricity">Electricity</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Guyana&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Electricity">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Electricity_sector_in_Guyana" title="Electricity sector in Guyana">Electricity sector in Guyana</a></div>\n<p>The electricity sector in Guyana is dominated by <a href="/wiki/Guyana_Power_and_Light" title="Guyana Power and Light">Guyana Power and Light</a> (GPL), the state-owned vertically integrated utility. Although the country has a large potential for hydroelectric and <a href="/wiki/Bagasse" title="Bagasse">bagasse</a>-fueled power generation, most of its 226 <a href="/wiki/Megawatt" class="mw-redirect" title="Megawatt">MW</a> of installed capacity correspond to inefficient diesel-engine driven generators.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (January 2012)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>\n</p><p>Several initiatives are in place to improve <a href="/wiki/Hinterland_energy_in_Guyana" title="Hinterland energy in Guyana">energy access in the hinterland</a>.\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Health">Health</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Guyana&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Health">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Health_in_Guyana" title="Health in Guyana">Health in Guyana</a></div>\n<p><a href="/wiki/Life_expectancy" title="Life expectancy">Life expectancy</a> at birth is estimated to be 67.39 years for both males and females in 2012.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> The PAHO/ WHO Global Health Report 2014 (using statistics of 2012) ranked the country as having the highest <a href="/wiki/Suicide" title="Suicide">suicide</a> rate in the world, with a mortality rate of 44.2 per 100,000 inhabitants.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup>  According to 2011 estimates from the <a href="/wiki/WHO" class="mw-redirect" title="WHO">WHO</a>, <a href="/wiki/HIV" title="HIV">HIV</a> <a href="/wiki/Prevalence" title="Prevalence">prevalence</a> is 1.2% of the teen/adult population (ages 15\xe2\x80\x9349).<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> Although Guyana\'s health profile falls short in comparison with many of its Caribbean neighbours, there has been remarkable progress since 1988, and the Ministry of Health is working to upgrade conditions, procedures, and facilities.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (January 2016)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Education">Education</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Guyana&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Education">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Education_in_Guyana" title="Education in Guyana">Education in Guyana</a></div>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Queens_College_Guyana.jpg" class="image"><img alt="Queens College Guyana.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/46/Queens_College_Guyana.jpg/220px-Queens_College_Guyana.jpg" width="220" height="167" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/46/Queens_College_Guyana.jpg/330px-Queens_College_Guyana.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/46/Queens_College_Guyana.jpg/440px-Queens_College_Guyana.jpg 2x" data-file-width="686" data-file-height="521" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Queens_College_Guyana.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div></div></div></div>\n<table class="plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Unreferenced" role="presentation"><tbody><tr><td class="mbox-image"><div style="width:52px"><a href="/wiki/File:Question_book-new.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/50px-Question_book-new.svg.png" width="50" height="39" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/75px-Question_book-new.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/100px-Question_book-new.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="512" data-file-height="399" /></a></div></td><td class="mbox-text"><div class="mbox-text-span">This section <b>does not <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citing_sources" title="Wikipedia:Citing sources">cite</a> any <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">sources</a></b>.<span class="hide-when-compact"> Please help <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Guyana&amp;action=edit">improve this section</a> by <a href="/wiki/Help:Introduction_to_referencing_with_Wiki_Markup/1" title="Help:Introduction to referencing with Wiki Markup/1">adding citations to reliable sources</a>. Unsourced material may be challenged and <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability#Burden_of_evidence" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">removed</a>.</span>  <small><i>(February 2013)</i></small><small class="hide-when-compact"><i> (<a href="/wiki/Help:Maintenance_template_removal" title="Help:Maintenance template removal">Learn how and when to remove this template message</a>)</i></small></div></td></tr></tbody></table>\n<p>Guyana\'s educational system is considered to be among the best in the Caribbean, but it deteriorated significantly in the 1980s, because of inadequate funding and emigration of many highly educated citizens. Although the education system recovered in the 1990s, it still does not produce the quality of educated students necessary for Guyana to modernise its workforce.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (May 2010)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> The country lacks a critical mass of expertise in many of the disciplines and activities on which it depends. At 88.5%, Guyana\'s literacy rate is the worst in South America.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>The educational system does not sufficiently focus on the training of Guyanese in science and technology, technical and vocational subjects, <a href="/wiki/Business_management" class="mw-redirect" title="Business management">business management</a>, or <a href="/wiki/Computer_science" title="Computer science">computer sciences</a>.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (May 2010)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> The Guyanese education system is modelled on the former <a href="/wiki/British_education" class="mw-redirect" title="British education">British education</a> system. Students are expected to take the NGSA (National Grade Six Assessment) for entrance into high school in grade 7. They take the <a href="/wiki/CXC" class="mw-redirect" title="CXC">CXC</a> at the end of high school. Schools have introduced the <a href="/wiki/Caribbean_Advanced_Proficiency_Examination" class="mw-redirect" title="Caribbean Advanced Proficiency Examination">CAPE</a> exams which all other Caribbean countries have introduced. The <a href="/wiki/Advanced_Level_(UK)" class="mw-redirect" title="Advanced Level (UK)">A-level</a> system, inherited from the British era, has all but disappeared and is offered only in a few schools.\n</p><p>Further adding to the problems of the educational system, many of the better-educated professional teachers have emigrated to other countries over the past two decades, mainly because of low pay, lack of opportunities and crime.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (May 2010)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Culture">Culture</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Guyana&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: Culture">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Culture_of_Guyana" title="Culture of Guyana">Culture of Guyana</a></div>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Literature_of_Guyana" class="mw-redirect" title="Literature of Guyana">Literature of Guyana</a> and <a href="/wiki/Music_of_Guyana" title="Music of Guyana">Music of Guyana</a></div>\n<table class="plainlinks metadata ambox ambox-content ambox-Unreferenced" role="presentation"><tbody><tr><td class="mbox-image"><div style="width:52px"><a href="/wiki/File:Question_book-new.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/50px-Question_book-new.svg.png" width="50" height="39" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/75px-Question_book-new.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/9/99/Question_book-new.svg/100px-Question_book-new.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="512" data-file-height="399" /></a></div></td><td class="mbox-text"><div class="mbox-text-span">This section <b>does not <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citing_sources" title="Wikipedia:Citing sources">cite</a> any <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">sources</a></b>.<span class="hide-when-compact"> Please help <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Guyana&amp;action=edit">improve this Unsourced material may be challenged and <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Verifiability#Burden_of_evidence" title="Wikipedia:Verifiability">removed</a>.</span>  <small><i>(February 2013)</i></small><small class="hide-when-compact"><i> (<a href="/wiki/Help:Maintenance_template_removal" title="Help:Maintenance template removal">Learn how and when to remove this template message</a>)</i></small></div></td></tr></tbody></table>\n<table style="float:right;" class="wikitable">\n<caption><span style="font-size:115%;">Holidays</span>\n</caption>\n<tbody><tr>\n<td>1 January</td>\n<td>New Year\'s Day\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>Spring</td>\n<td><a href="/wiki/Youman_Nabi" class="mw-redirect" title="Youman Nabi">Youman Nabi</a> (Mawlid)\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>23 February</td>\n<td><a href="/wiki/Republic_Day" title="Republic Day">Republic Day</a>&#160;/&#32;<a href="/wiki/Mashramani" title="Mashramani">Mashramani</a>\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>March</td>\n<td><a href="/wiki/Phagwah" class="mw-redirect" title="Phagwah">Phagwah</a>\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>March&#160;/&#32;April</td>\n<td><a href="/wiki/Good_Friday" title="Good Friday">Good Friday</a>\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>March&#160;/&#32;April</td>\n<td><a href="/wiki/Easter_Sunday" class="mw-redirect" title="Easter Sunday">Easter Sunday</a>\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>1 May</td>\n<td><a href="/wiki/Labour_Day" title="Labour Day">Labour Day</a>\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>5 May</td>\n<td><a href="/wiki/Indian_Arrival_Day" title="Indian Arrival Day">Indian Arrival Day</a>\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>26 May</td>\n<td><a href="/wiki/Independence_Day" class="mw-redirect" title="Independence Day">Independence Day</a>\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>First Monday in July</td>\n<td><a href="/wiki/CARICOM_Day" class="mw-redirect" title="CARICOM Day">CARICOM Day</a>\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>1 August</td>\n<td><a href="/wiki/Emancipation_Day" title="Emancipation Day">Emancipation Day</a>\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>October&#160;/&#32;November</td>\n<td><a href="/wiki/Diwali" title="Diwali">Diwali</a>\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td>25 December</td>\n<td>Christmas\n</td></tr>\n<tr>\n<td><span class="nowrap">26 or 27 December</span></td>\n<td><a href="/wiki/Boxing_Day" title="Boxing Day">Boxing Day</a>\n</td></tr></tbody></table>\n<p>Guyana\'s culture is very similar to that of the English-speaking Caribbean, and has historically been tied to the English-speaking Caribbean as part of the British Empire when it became a possession in the nineteenth century. Guyana is a founding member of the <a href="/wiki/Caricom" class="mw-redirect" title="Caricom">Caricom</a> (Caribbean Community) economic bloc and also the home of the Bloc\'s Headquarters, the CARICOM Secretariat.\n</p><p>Guyana\'s geographical location, its sparsely populated rain-forest regions, and its substantial Amerindian population differentiate it from English-speaking Caribbean countries. Its blend of Indo-Guyanese (East Indian) and Afro-Guyanese (African) cultures gives it similarities to <a href="/wiki/Trinidad" title="Trinidad">Trinidad</a> and distinguishes it from other parts of the Americas. Guyana shares similar interests with the islands in the West Indies, such as food, festive events, music, sports, etc.\n</p><p>Guyana plays international cricket as a part of the <a href="/wiki/West_Indian_cricket_team" class="mw-redirect" title="West Indian cricket team">West Indies cricket team</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/Guyanese_cricket_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Guyanese cricket team">Guyana team</a> plays <a href="/wiki/First_class_cricket" class="mw-redirect" title="First class cricket">first-class cricket</a> against other nations of the Caribbean. In March and April 2007 Guyana co-hosted the <a href="/wiki/Cricket_World_Cup_2007" class="mw-redirect" title="Cricket World Cup 2007">Cricket World Cup 2007</a>. In addition to its CARICOM membership, Guyana is a member of <a href="/wiki/CONCACAF" title="CONCACAF">CONCACAF</a>, the international football federation for North and Central America and the Caribbean.\n</p><p>Events include <a href="/wiki/Mashramani" title="Mashramani">Mashramani</a> (Mash), <a href="/wiki/Phagwah" class="mw-redirect" title="Phagwah">Phagwah</a> (<a href="/wiki/Holi" title="Holi">Holi</a>), and <a href="/wiki/Deepavali" class="mw-redirect" title="Deepavali">Deepavali</a> (<a href="/wiki/Diwali" title="Diwali">Diwali</a>).\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Wildlife">Wildlife</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Guyana&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Wildlife">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<p>Among the birds found on Guyana is cock of the rock (<i><a href="/wiki/Rupicola_rupicola" class="mw-redirect" title="Rupicola rupicola">Rupicola rupicola</a></i>).<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Sports">Sports</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Guyana&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Sports">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Cricket_in_the_West_Indies" title="Cricket in the West Indies">Cricket in the West Indies</a></div>\n<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Providence_Stadium_outside.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4c/Providence_Stadium_outside.jpg/220px-Providence_Stadium_outside.jpg" width="220" height="122" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4c/Providence_Stadium_outside.jpg/330px-Providence_Stadium_outside.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4c/Providence_Stadium_outside.jpg/440px-Providence_Stadium_outside.jpg 2x" data-file-width="931" data-file-height="516" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Providence_Stadium_outside.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Providence Stadium as seen from the East Bank Highway</div></div></div>\n<p>The major sports in Guyana are <a href="/wiki/Guyana_national_cricket_team" title="Guyana national cricket team">cricket</a> (Guyana is part of the West Indies as defined for international cricket purposes<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup>), <a href="/wiki/Basketball_in_Guyana" title="Basketball in Guyana">basketball</a>, <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">football (soccer)</a>, and volleyball.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> Minor sports include <a href="/wiki/Beach_cricket" class="mw-redirect" title="Beach cricket">softball cricket (beach cricket)</a>, field hockey, <a href="/wiki/Netball" title="Netball">netball</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rounders" title="Rounders">rounders</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lawn_tennis" class="mw-redirect" title="Lawn tennis">lawn tennis</a>,  table tennis, <a href="/wiki/Boxing" title="Boxing">boxing</a>, <a href="/wiki/Squash_(sport)" title="Squash (sport)">squash</a>, <a href="/wiki/Guyana_national_rugby_union_team" title="Guyana national rugby union team">rugby</a>, <a href="/wiki/Horse_racing" title="Horse racing">horse racing</a> and a few others.\n</p><p>Guyana played host to <a href="/wiki/International_cricket" title="International cricket">international cricket</a> matches as part of the <a href="/wiki/2007_Cricket_World_Cup" title="2007 Cricket World Cup">2007 Cricket World Cup</a> (CWC 2007). The new 15,000-seat Providence Stadium, also referred to as Guyana National Stadium, was built in time for the World Cup and was ready for the beginning of play on 28 March. At the first international game of CWC 2007 at the stadium, <a href="/wiki/Lasith_Malinga" title="Lasith Malinga">Lasith Malinga</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Sri_Lanka_national_cricket_team" title="Sri Lanka national cricket team">Sri Lankan team</a> took four wickets in four consecutive deliveries.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>For international football purposes, <a href="/wiki/Guyana_national_football_team" title="Guyana national football team">Guyana</a> is part of CONCACAF. The highest league in their club system is the <a href="/wiki/GFF_Elite_League" title="GFF Elite League">GFF Elite League</a>.\n</p><p>Guyana also has five courses for horse racing.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<div style="clear:both;"></div>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="See_also">See also</span><span Christians.</span>\n</li>\n</ol></div>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="References">References</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a
